'''
O in aug-cc-pV9Z
'''

import pyscf
from pyscf.gto.basis import parse_gaussian

mol = pyscf.M(
    atom = '''       
        O
    ''',
    unit = 'angstrom',
    basis = {
            'O' : parse_gaussian.load('/home/nike/AI_ENERGIES/O/av9z.gbs', 'O')
    },
    charge = 0,
    spin = 2,
    verbose = 9,
    symmetry = True,
    output = 'O_av9z.txt',
    symmetry_subgroup = 'Dooh',
)

#mol.max_memory =100000
#mol.max_memory =16000
mol.max_memory =4000
#mol.max_memory =100
#mf = mol.ROHF()
mf = mol.UHF()
mf.irrep_nelec = {'A1g': (2,2), 'E1ux': (1,0), 'E1uy': (1,0),'A1u': (1,1)}
#mf.irrep_nelec = {'A1g': 4, 'E1ux': 1, 'E1uy': 1,'A1u': 2}
mf.chkfile = 'O_av9z.chk'
mf.init_guess='atom'
#mf.init_guess='O_av7z_UHF.chk'
mf.kernel()
